Trial Winning Decklists
=======================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on September 15, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











A total of 29 Modern Grand Prix Trials took place yesterday, granting their respective winners two round byes in the main event today. The hottest archetypes were 5-Color Humans and Bant Spirits but a healthy range of archetypes were represented. Without further ado, let's take a look at all 29 decklists!
